The “American Indian Heritage Day in Texas” is celebrating its 5th Anniversary of the State Observance Law in Texas on September 30, 2017 at the Lone Star Park in Grand Prairie, Texas. We are focusing on the rich culture and preservation of the Five Civilized Tribes. We are very excited to work with the Choctaw Nation of Oklahoma in making this year’s theme “Echoes of (Tru)th” a success. This celebration gives us an opportunity to share our knowledge. With Choctaw Nation alliance, we can bring a new forward thinking to educate a new audience, a new generation and non-Indians . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . + Friday, September 29, 2017 + Educational Observance Day in the State of Texas is a day for public schools, organizations, and businesses. The morning presentation will highlight a very challenging topic, “American Indian Stickball - The creation of the game and the forerunner to Lacrosse”. We are introducing the Southeastern Style of the Game. The noon presentation will be Tribal Connection whereby recognition of tribal dignitaries, Strikingsticks Award and the honoring of the Elder of the Year. The afternoon presentation will be a discussion on “The Five Civilized Tribes - Sacredness of Tribal Songs and Social Dances”. The songs will focus on the church hymns sung with tribal dialect, stomp dance songs and social dance songs. केली आहे. यंदाचं कार्यक्रम Bartlett High School ला दिनांक २ सप्टेंबरला होईल आणि  यावर्षी आपल्याकडे येणार आहेत, प्रख्यात गायक आणि (BMM मधला कल्लोळ पाहिल्यानंतर तिळमात्रही संशय न घेता) अभिनेते राहुल देशपांडे. राहुलची सुरली मैफिल यावेळच्या गणपतीच्या कार्यक्रमाला अविस्मरणीय करेल यात शंकाच नाही. राहुलने आपल्या सर्वाना एक आपुलकीचं आणि आग्रहाचं आमंत्रण दिले आहे, या संकेतस्थळावर टिचकी मारा
